rgb>“对其本国已往历史有一种温情与敬意，至少不会对其本国已往历史抱一种偏激的虚无主义，亦至少不会感到现在我们是站在已往历史最高之顶点，而将我们当身种种罪恶与弱点，一切诿卸于古人。”</span></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, rgb><br></span></strong></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">1939年，钱穆写下这段话时中国正值生死存亡的至暗时刻。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">八十多年过去了，我们正在向着光明的未来不断攀登，本国的历史就像留在地上的影子，越拉越长，不断变换着姿态。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">诚然，历史已成过往。用现代的人角度去看古代，不顺眼的事情太多；用现代人的标准去评判古人，“落后”的地方俯拾皆是。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">古人又不会辩解，只能默默挨批。历史又不会言语，只能寄希望于他人理解。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">一个家族一路走来尚且免不了磕磕绊绊，更何况一个历经数千年文明的大国？地理是历史的舞台，中国的历史是由生活在这片土地上的人共同书写的，我们也只是其中的惊鸿一瞥。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(190, 26, 29);\">钱穆反复强调</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">，站在现代的角度审判过往的历史，将我们身上的种种弱点推诿于古人，并不是大国国民对待历史的正确态度。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">自始至终，</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(190, 26, 29);\">历史研习社都希望怀抱温情与敬意</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">，从学术的视野出发，讲述不一样的中国历史故事：王朝权力更迭的逻辑、草原部落强盛的密码、决定天下大势的地理枢纽、北上南下的交通节点、帝王的财富攫取之道……</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">如此深厚的历史沉淀，数千年延绵不绝的的文明史，对于我们来说应该是一种荣耀。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">阅读历史就要神游冥想，在古人身处的具体情境中看尽长河落日。</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">八千里路云和月，一篇读罢头飞雪，如此而已。<br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\">——————————————————<br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><br></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">出版社设计了六款候选封面</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">底图是《平番得胜图》</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">颜色有三种</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">淡黄色走清新路线</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">深浅两种红色突出历史厚重感<br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">请大家一起来帮帮忙，</span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;\">根据封面需要投票选出自己心目中的最佳设计吧！<br></span></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 1.75em;letter-spacing: 1px;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);font-size: 17px;\">一、顺德人对吃的讲究</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p></section></section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">要想知道顺德人对吃为什么这么挑剔，得先从顺德人的饮食习惯聊起。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">顺德人的一天，往往从一碗热气腾腾的粥开始。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6657407407407407\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aZdMAw7z1e7ticS3VDTf2PvHgib1C8ztP9Tr6HpTuZ5YFoc5nl9SRUR1Q/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">对一般人来说，喝粥嘛有啥好讲究的？不就是简单的白米粥嘛？就算是要讲究一点，撑死也就加点皮蛋瘦肉啥的顶头了。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">但是顺德人可不，花样可多了。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">有</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">窝蛋牛肉粥</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，在白粥滚开时倒入腌好的牛肉片，出锅后还得下一枚新鲜的生鸡蛋，借余热烫熟，搅碎金黄；</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">有</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">生滚鱼片粥</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，除在粥中加入鲩鱼鱼片之外，还得配以生菜，香菇、芹菜、香菜等诸多蔬菜才算正宗。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6666666666666666\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aYcKv6pLExTyQfsre6ADtXZ7DIaq5wRW9RJl8nyMAwBgfOrAU98Yibww/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">有</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">猪杂粥</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，经过调制后的猪杂，在严苛的火候下与滚烫的白粥“风云际会”，猪脑细腻、猪肚缠绵、猪肝香脆，都在一锅之中“兼容并包”。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">更有创意突破天际的</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">毋米粥</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，以香米煮至烂熟，去粒而存浆，加鸡汤调味熬出汤底。食用时如同吃火锅一样，将从山珍到海味的各类食材放入其中涮涮食用。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6666666666666666\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aGs5pJ3aSB1amVr3a4rmBN7qyN9cGObUMNeOkXPBibPfvlZrxeq7jYfg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">待到食材倾尽，只剩一锅浓汤之时，再舀入碗中细细品味。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">区区一碗粥，被顺德人魔改到这份上，已经让人搞不清顺德人到底是在吃火锅还是在吃粥了。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">被顺德人玩坏的不仅有粥，还有牛奶。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">比如</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">广式甜品双皮奶</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">的大名可谓是无人不知无人不晓。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6666666666666666\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06a3rJ3PA2AGwjp3q33IpxKttGoEJB9JfeylU2fltywC1KE7YPjW5Q1vQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">据说双皮奶的诞生，完全是由于清末顺德人的一次无心之举。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">在一次意外中，顺德人发现本地富含乳脂的水牛奶停止加热后，在与空气接触迅速冷却的过程中，会结成了一层厚厚的奶皮。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">而将奶液翻滚把奶皮压下，等第二层奶皮浮现时，这一碗牛奶会变得无比的香醇浓厚。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">于是发现了新大陆的顺德人马上脑洞大开的将魔改之手伸向了牛奶。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6675925925925926\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aFrbLj44woKIwZqkRpTGOEEq0EYd80BSq4MKEWCBj2Ew0fzRlQSQORA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">加热、冷却、去奶留皮、奶液打入蛋清、加入白糖、倒回碗中奶皮上浮……每一步的时机、温度、用量，都随着奶的状态变化。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">通过一代代顺德人的魔改，双皮奶终于横空出世，并凭借其弹嫩的口感与浓郁的风味征服大江南北，受到无数人的追捧。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">当然，如同对粥的魔改没有止境一样，顺德人对牛奶的魔改也并未因双皮奶而止步。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">有在严格温控之下以姜汁和牛奶调配的</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">姜撞奶</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">；有以奶入粥的</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">奶滚粥</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">；还有魔改到极致的</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">炒牛奶</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">了。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.499074074074074\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06a7Vias6IfV96FqJwDdnp5VQcJPUnic52WKP2BJC2fX5wIwEJnmNUhzc2A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">所谓炒牛奶，是以牛奶混合蛋清与适量生粉，以及蟹子、虾仁和榄仁等配料。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">下锅后下锅不断搅拌，一方面要控制火候温度，增一分则易焦糊，减一分则难成型；</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">另一方面得长时间旋转，一铲一推，约略九次才炒成半凝固状态，看着像一堆松垮的土豆泥。但入口却缠绵馥郁，回味无穷。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.5\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aoeias1X1k1hn1ZQSUBV0XyknnXNVhP466QSWCib2TibvtKQa8moMuVaYA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">能把牛奶玩成土豆泥，也只有顺德这帮魔改厨子能干得出来。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><section><section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 17px;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 17px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">二、“生鱼片”也是中国的，更是顺德的</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p></section></section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">当然，顺德人可不仅仅只是魔改，他们也在无意中保留了一些我们中华民族的传统美食，比如生鱼片。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6675925925925926\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06ahXLZGTIW8L9pUHOaibu7USH8z7XrPQiaxKiaBbeEniao2eKJ4X6sSoZmEg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">每每谈到生鱼片，大家的第一反应大多都是看上去逼格满满的日本料理。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">但是，其实日本这道菜，也是跟我们大中华偷师的。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">只不过后来我们自己渐渐把生鱼片这道菜忘了，反而日本拿着这道菜在全世界打响了名头。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">但是在顺德，还保留了我大中华的这道传统美食，而且无论是做工还是口味，都比山寨版的日本生鱼片要好不少。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6657407407407407\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aKo5QuMsM3y5CqNmSPktvtyP8G0m970HVs0Kia9WbF03ialmN3tOnuPnQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">顺德的生鱼片，无疑是最接近鲜之本味的吃鱼方式。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">一尾活鱼取肉，以精湛刀法剔骨去刺，切成几可透光的薄片，叠成花瓣状置于冰盘上，故又称</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">“菊花鱼生”</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">最为传统的吃法只加以油、盐调味，保留了鱼肉的肥美嫩滑。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">顺德人吃鱼生的时候要有个“捞起”的动作，代表着“越捞越旺”、“风生水起”，鱼生入口绵柔，回味鲜甜，浑如“天然去雕饰”的素颜美人，顺德鱼生光配料就有十几种。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6796296296296296\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aziaT0fEYjO4A7fjI9mp4mYeRoPPJx2Z1ouvv7vsjmLUE0H9fcbk8Igg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">吃鱼生前，先根据个人喜好挑好配料，加以油、盐、糖，和冰好的鱼生一起在碗里拌一拌，然后立马将鱼生佐料调料一口吃进嘴里，仔细咀嚼，各式香、辛、酸、甜的佐料将鱼生之鲜美尽情带出，使得满口溢香，无穷回味，叫人欲罢不能。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">相较而言，日本人只会以芥末酱油为调料，就显得单调多了。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">此外，日本人吃鱼生以厚切为主，因为这样能充分体现原料的最佳味道。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">而在顺德就不一样了，顺德鱼生是一道非常考验师傅刀工的功夫菜，一个好的师傅，能把鱼片切成仅0.5毫米左右的厚度，薄如蝉翼，晶莹剔透，漂亮至极。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6666666666666666\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06aapwIs3L5zMOFz14ibx6FVAPiciapbO21ibL0UZmTCiaRvAZxuOL94kp7Sibg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">顺德人好吃鱼，在这上面花的心思也多，除了生鱼片之外，鱼头可以炖，鱼皮可以凉拌，还有鱼皮饺，可谓是五花八门。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><section><section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 17px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">三、顺德的厨子</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p></section></section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">顺德人对于吃既然如此讲究，其厨艺自然也是天下闻名，自古就有</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">“吃在广州，厨出凤城”</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">之说。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">自清末民初以来，凤城厨师挟技出外闯世界，他们前往穗、港、澳，以至东南亚及欧、美、非洲开餐馆酒楼，把顺德菜用为粤菜的代表推向全球，所以，“在海外，顺德饭馆每每是粤菜会所”，许多饭店冠以“凤城厨师主理”的招牌以广招来客。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.4981273408239701\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1068\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06apOX3wGAgOia3b9sPibvDmg3aa6Opibjibblypvbpgj98FqXwxG3kKibnKzA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">20世纪初，部分自梳女到广州、香港、新加坡等地做女佣，这些“顺德妈姐”精于烹饪，广州西关美食，其实便是她们的遗制。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">时至今日，在美食之风的熏陶下，顺德几乎人人皆厨，个个都喜欢下厨来几下。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">以纵横的水网为筋骨，肥沃的土壤为躯体，世代的传承为血脉，飘荡的乡愁为记忆，顺德“全民皆厨”，虽并非是人人都掌勺，然而饮食确实是他们的一门“家学”。</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6675925925925926\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/MzRQwBpUAMIWnCpkCCJCxNBS1XF2ib06a7JKNZIEYGV9nCJRuc21VRDLeRzIKRf28JmxicLkH1Va0Xib7l3lbiaWHQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">所以，看似吃饭挑剔，其实是他们内心深处对家乡的那份不变的眷恋，顺德人口味的挑剔，完完全全就是被他们老家那种对食材的讲究给惯出来的。</span></p><p><br></p><section data-darkmode-bgcolor-15957462478704=\"rgb(25, 25, 25)\" data-darkmode-original-bgcolor-15957462478704=\"rgb(255, 255, 255)\" data-darkmode-color-15957462478704=\"rgba(163, 163, 163, 0.8)\" data-darkmode-original-color-15957462478704=\"rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)\" data-style=\"padding-right: 16px; padding-left: 16px; white-space: normal; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8); font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif letter-spacing: background-color: rgb background-repeat: repeat background-position: left top background-size: auto overflow-wrap: break-word 25)\" data-darkmode-original-bgcolor-15961912350444=\"rgb(255, 255, 255)\" data-darkmode-color-15961912350444=\"rgb(136, 136, 136)\" data-darkmode-original-color-15961912350444=\"rgb(136, 136, 136)\" !important;\">  </span><span data-darkmode-bgcolor-15958384301416=\"rgb(25, 25, 25)\" data-darkmode-original-bgcolor-15958384301416=\"rgb(255, 255, 255)\" data-darkmode-color-15958384301416=\"rgb(136,
