!important;\"> 审核：徐飞   编排：汤圆</span></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">七月七日长生殿，夜半无人私语时。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\">在七夕佳节，唐玄宗和杨贵妃的情爱故事成为仅次于牛郎织女的谈资。</span><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\">但两人爱情故事的社会评价却走过了一千多年相当波折的路。</span><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"> </span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 17px;\">一、丑闻</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 17px;\"><br></span></strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">尽管唐玄宗杨贵妃的情爱已经是家喻户晓，但我们依然有必要重温一下。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">开元二十五年，西元737年，亲手缔造了开元盛世的唐玄宗李隆基在情路上遇到了一次重大挫折：心爱的武惠妃辞世，享年约四十岁。为此，皇帝闷闷不乐，以至于伤心欲绝，而当时后宫佳丽不可胜数，却难以使皇帝转忧为喜。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">驸马都尉杨洄，看出了玄宗的心事，就与宦官高力士商量，寻机向皇帝进言惠妃的儿媳、寿王李瑁妃杨氏「姿质天挺，宜充掖廷」。于是皇帝打算将杨氏召入后宫之中。这杨氏，小字玉环，蒲州永乐（今山西永济）人。父杨玄琰，蜀州司户。两年前玉环嫁给寿王，夫妻感情尚笃。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">无论古今中外，女子嫁父子二人，都被认为是乱伦</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，此前类似的丑事还发生在武媚娘先后侍奉太宗和高宗爷俩身上，骆宾王曾痛斥武氏「陷吾君于聚麀」（鹿之父子可共享一母鹿）。但</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">玄宗的手下还是想了一个「聚麀」的办法</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">——</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t《新唐书》载，开元二十八年（740年）十月，以为皇帝母亲窦太后祈福的名义，敕书寿王妃杨氏出家为女道士，道号「太真」。据考证，杨太真正式入道时间是开元二十九年正月二日。至天宝三载，杨氏身份为女道士。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4185185185185185\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38); font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light; font-size: 15px; letter-spacing: 1px; white-space: normal; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQseSwZXjNO01y3BQMKGnHyUkgC6XDcz5yZVPNdb3Qg8VTlBwficTeCbb5g/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t四载（745）七月，李瑁新娶韦氏。八月，杨太真受册封为贵妃，为玄宗妃嫔中地位最高者。此时杨氏二十七岁，而唐玄宗已六十一岁了，杨氏反成为李瑁的庶母。</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">杨氏被宫人呼为「娘子」，礼数实同于皇后。</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t杨贵妃受宠幸，族人也随之鸡犬升天，「姊妹弟兄皆列土，可怜光彩生门户」，烜赫一时。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t杨氏家族飞扬跋扈、胡作非为，朝野均对他们充满了巨大的怨恨，唐朝政治更加腐败。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t不过，天宝五载，杨贵妃闹出了被遣送回娘家的丑剧。还是高力士察言观色，不久之后就把杨氏迎回。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t渔阳鼙鼓动地来，惊破霓裳羽衣曲，天宝十四载（755）冬，范阳、平卢、河东三镇节度使安禄山以清君侧，反杨国忠为名起兵叛乱，兵锋西指长安。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t次年，皇帝带着杨贵妃与杨国忠等人逃往蜀中，途经马嵬驿（今陕西兴平西）时，陈玄礼为首的随驾禁军军士哗变，将杨国忠寸斩。唐玄宗赞扬军士为国除奸，但陈将军等力主处决杨氏。</span><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);font-size: 15px;\">皇帝为求自保，不得已赐杨贵妃白绫一条，缢死在佛堂的梨树下，年三十八。</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;line-height: normal;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-croporisrc=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQsedvJ5MrILh6gib9SR2yZvKYUtGPyibIKx1gVfjpg2pjw2ClhHqhRUe7FQ/0?wx_fmt=jpeg\" data-cropx1=\"0\" data-cropx2=\"1080\" data-cropy1=\"75.16483516483517\" data-cropy2=\"534.0659340659341\" data-ratio=\"0.42407407407407405\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"width: 546px; height: 232px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQse5ibKSvgp9MpzLbxFk0yt2p3V84ZYSEyXXhjJVmxibRw3icgWkF0r78mNQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">▲《妖猫传》中杨贵妃自愿接受“尸解大法”的谎言</span></section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t总结下唐玄宗杨贵妃的故事，可以用</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">丑、丑、丑</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">来形容：李隆基乱伦为一丑；随意遣返杨氏为二丑；马嵬之变丢卒保车为第三丑。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"> </span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);font-size: 17px;\"><strong>二、唐人·批判</strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">安史之乱是李唐王朝的转折点，唐人每每念此，无不唏嘘，多痛恨玄宗荒淫误国。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">亲历丧乱者杜工部在《哀江头》中直面了惨状，又叹息：「明眸皓齿今何在？血污游魂归不得！」</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">中唐的白居易，有《长恨歌</span></strong><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">》</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。表面是说「汉皇重色思倾国，御宇多年求不得」，但实则是借汉喻唐，委婉地表示了愤懑。不过，诗歌的后半还是寄托在「虚无缥缈间」，说是杨贵妃和李隆基能「天上人间会相见」，盟誓互不相弃。最后说：</span><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\">在天愿作比翼鸟，在地愿为连理枝。天长地久有时尽，此恨绵绵无绝期。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">用「长恨」表达了李杨的悲剧，实则也是大唐的悲剧。</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.4166666666666667\" data-type=\"other\" data-w=\"1080\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQseVy16CEccGaqf23lXYrF05bRMic2kjSS7Ulia3VcZiaicibYiabNSddUMvWvA/640?wx_fmt=other\" style=\"max-width: 600px\"></section><section style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;font-size: 12px;letter-spacing: 1px;text-align: center;\">▲《妖猫传》中黄轩饰演的白居易正在创作《长恨歌》</span></section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">如果白居易还算是宽容，那晚唐的李义山对于唐玄宗则充满了鞭挞，其《马嵬二首》毫不客气，如其二：</span><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\">海外徒闻更九州岛，他生未卜此生休。空闻虎旅传宵柝，无复鸡人报晓筹。此日六军同驻马，当时七夕笑牵牛。如何四纪为天子，不及卢家有莫愁。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">万恶淫为首，大家李隆基竟然把自己奋斗出来的盛世打得粉碎，留下了多少遗憾！</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">杜牧更是在《过华清宫绝句三首》中表达了讽喻，如其一：</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">长安回望绣成堆，山顶千门次第开。一骑红尘妃子笑，无人知是荔枝来。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">罗隐最不客气，《马嵬坡》直陈玄宗为美色所惑，破家亡身：</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">佛屋前头野草春，贵妃轻骨此为尘。从来绝色知难得，不破中原未是人。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">我们可知，</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">晚唐以后，文人对于唐玄宗的评价从感伤转为批判，他们痛斥他的荒淫葬送了帝国。</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"> </span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 17px;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">三、大宋：殷鉴</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">五代的刘昫在《唐书》中规</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">避了唐玄宗乱伦的丑事，说天宝危机是「用人之失也」。</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t不过，大宋则对李杨故事发表了很多批判，尤其是在六一居士等人修的《新唐书》中有这样的点评：</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">「玄宗亲平其乱，可以鉴矣，而又败以女子。……及侈心一动，穷天下之欲不足为其乐，而溺其所甚爱，忘其所可戒，至于窜身失国而不悔。考其始终之异，其性习之相远也至于如此。可不慎哉！可不慎哉！」</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\">以李隆基为殷鉴，告诫官家不要再犯类似荒淫失国的错误。</span><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">市民意识兴起的宋朝坊间，又是如何看待前朝呢？</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">乐史有《杨太真外传》两卷，综合了唐、五代所作诗歌、笔记和小说中有关李杨故事和传说，特别是有关杨玉环之事巨细毕载，可谓杨妃遗闻轶事的集大成之作。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">宋、金对峙，</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">在汴梁和临安等地热闹非凡的瓦舍勾栏里，「说话人」也有讲说李杨爱情故事的</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。从罗烨《醉翁谈录》传奇类中有《花萼楼》的书目，可见端倪。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><img data-ratio=\"1.25\" data-type=\"other\" data-w=\"1080\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQsenv5xKXDsgYfc0kvOuY4icmFBPosvfIHKjees5l1A5WDeyiaFQWmH1OPQ/640?wx_fmt=other\" style=\"max-width: 600px\"></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t在当时「说话人」的重要参考书《绿窗新话》中，就集录了不少有关李杨爱情故事的传奇作品。如《杨贵妃私通安禄山》、《杨贵妃窃宁王玉笛》、《杨贵妃舞霓裳曲》、《唐明皇咽助情花》、《明皇爱花奴羯鼓》、《虢国夫人自有美艳》和《永新娘最号善歌》等。与此同时，有关李杨的爱情故事也已被编成戏文、院本，开始在舞台上演唱了。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t看来，有宋一代，对于李杨故事，</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\"><strong>官方较为严肃批评，而民间则是猎奇为主</strong></span><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">——这和市民化进程加快不无关联。</span></p><p>\t</p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 17px;\"><strong><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">四、蒙元：同情  </span></strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">蒙治时期，仕途经济无路之书会才人逐渐选择去拥抱市民。杂剧的勃兴，在某种意义上将原本对李杨的批判扭转为同情，最早的是涿州人王伯成的</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">《天宝遗事诸宫调》</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t作品叙述李杨爱情以及安史之乱致的生离死别；其间有对李、杨悲剧命运的同情，亦有对杨玉环、安禄山「私情暗通」的谴责，还含有对玄宗无道的批判，思想内容较为复杂，文辞则以典雅流畅见长。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">从总的倾向来看，王伯成对玄宗尚为同情理解，对杨妃则持批评态度</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。若与其杂剧 《李太白贬夜郎》 联系起来看，两者的思想倾向是一致的。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t然而，真正把同情作为主旋律的，无疑是白朴的</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">《唐明皇秋夜梧桐雨》</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">《元曲选》中此剧题目：</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\">安禄山反叛兵戈举</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t陈玄礼拆散鸾凤侣</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">正名为：</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t杨贵妃晓日荔枝香</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t唐明皇秋夜梧桐雨</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t全剧略去了梅妃江采苹的关目，也未写李杨在月宫的重圆，而以唐明皇的长恨作结。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">《梧桐雨》</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">是以唐明皇为主唱角的末本戏(正末主唱)，剧中虽也暴露了唐明皇因歌舞坏江山，且对此不无谴责。但是，作者抨击的矛头是指向在入侵者面前显得束手无策的文武两班。剧作充分肯定了玄宗对于爱情的执着，歌颂了他对杨妃的生死不渝。为了减轻皇帝对安史之乱应负的严重责任，以加强人们对他的同情，白朴已经加入了玄宗自我忏悔的桥段。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><img data-ratio=\"0.687037037037037\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQseuseKbfPo0LFlBhULHpgZZryF2ficF3NqxE1eAhAOq8Be6XNAib5k2DOA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\" style=\"max-width: 600px\"></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">《梧桐雨》中的唐明皇，带有更多的历史真实性，因而也显得更为具体、鲜明。这是与《长恨歌》不同的地方，也是戏剧形式较之七言诗歌能更好地创造人物形象的表现。原因在于白朴既有「当日多情属帝家」的思想，又寄托自己的故国之思。众所周知，在蒙古的黑暗殖民统治之下，人们同情李杨，往往是民族意识的一种曲折的反映。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">《梧桐雨》细致地刻划唐明皇的内心世界，使他成为一个有个性的悲剧形象；比较成功地创造了符合剧情发展需要的悲剧气氛；加上情节线索分明，结构谨严，戏剧语言优美动人，</span><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\"><strong>特别是第四折中那种撼人心灵的抒情独唱</strong></span><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，不愧为一部优秀的剧作——</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">【黄钟煞】顺西风低把纱窗哨，送寒气频将绣户敲。莫不是天故半人愁闷搅？前度铃声响栈道。似花奴羯鼓调，如伯牙《水仙操》。洗黄花润篱落，渍苍苔倒墙角。渲湖山漱石窍，浸枯荷溢池沼。沾残蝶粉渐消，洒流萤焰不着。绿窗前促织叫，声相近雁影高。催邻砧处处捣，助新凉分外早。斟量来这一宵，雨和人紧厮熬。伴铜壶点点敲，雨更多泪不少。雨湿寒梢，泪染龙袍。不肯相饶。共隔着一树梧桐直滴到晓。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t此剧在历代评价甚高，李调元《雨村曲话》说：</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">「元人咏马嵬事无虑数十家，白仁甫《梧桐雨》剧为最」</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。王国维《人间词话》说：「白仁甫《秋夜梧桐雨》剧，沈雄悲壮，为元曲冠冕。」</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"> </span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);font-size: 17px;\"><strong>五、明朝：惊鸿</strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">明代，李杨故事仍旧是戏剧创作的重要题材之一，令人遗憾的是，除《彩毫记》和《惊鸿记》之外，其余各本均已失传了。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">吴世美的</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">《惊鸿记》</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，创作主要目的是</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">「看往代荒淫败乱，今朝垂戒词场」</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">，主写李、杨和梅妃之间的三角恋爱，自始至终并列地描写了梅妃和杨妃的失宠得幸，生离死别。整个剧作情节庞杂，头绪纷繁。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">吴世美认为女人是祸国殃民的「祸水」，在剧中，</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">杨贵妃成为争风吃醋的悍妇；又点明她原是寿王之妃，且与安禄山有私情</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。因此，杨贵妃和李隆基根本谈不上有爱情，其不惜一切地与梅妃争宠，只是为了保持她那种荒淫无耻的享乐生活。对于被诬遭贬的梅妃，作者似乎较同情，作为红颜薄命的牺牲者，最后还让她与唐明皇团圆。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><section style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\"><img data-ratio=\"0.5611111111111111\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"900\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQseMPEibXxrUWxpteVAEnKtG4ibFKQzcVpSbnNmTQ0vScbJ16bL4koGwrjw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\" style=\"max-width: 600px\"></span></section><section style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: normal;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">▲《大唐荣耀》中刻画的安禄山形象</span></section><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">吴世美笔下的唐明皇，是个风流好色的昏君。他心中始终有着杨、梅两妃，既与江采苹有梅亭私誓，又与杨玉环结七夕之盟；而当杨妃惨死、梅妃失踪后，他都思念，显而易见，李隆基「你不懂爱」。末出《幽明大会》中，作者还让杨、梅都作了真诚忏悔。一个说：「早知别离永相忆，谁待要生时妒取。」一个道：「奴家亦思玉妃，恨不即死。」十分有趣。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t大明商品经济发达，文化消费意识渐增，故作家主动去迎合受众，表现出了大相径庭的艺术旨趣，故对于李杨故事不能概论。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"> </span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: center;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(171, 25, 66);font-size: 17px;\"><strong>六、满清：讴歌</strong></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(38, 38, 38);font-size: 15px;\">甲申国难后，异族用四十年的时间再次控制了中国全境……</span><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t在江南，天才剧作家</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">洪昇</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">横空出世。偶然的机会，他萌发了为李杨写一部纯粹传奇的想法，</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">「凡史家秽语，概削不书」</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t洪昇充实了《长恨歌》诗、传的内容，把李杨情爱发挥到了极致，定名为《长生殿》。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t这部佳作的高妙就在</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">于写帝王情感而又不限于此，天上人间熔于一炉，把原本招人非议的皇室丑闻化为至情至性的真挚爱情。</span></strong></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t在洪昇的笔下，帝王也如百姓一般有自己的爱恨情仇；同时，从戏曲角度说，避免了《梧桐雨》刻画马嵬之变的悲伤凄绝，让李杨能在天上重圆，不留遗憾的“长生”也暗合了传统戏剧精神的中和之美。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><img data-croporisrc=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQsegOYCHhechAd1Eq1TFVK9sib7hRIcSu7iaUfQtJmmCOAHtMjCejQK6KZw/0?wx_fmt=other\" data-cropx1=\"0\" data-cropx2=\"1080\" data-cropy1=\"73.1868131868132\" data-cropy2=\"536.0439560439561\" data-ratio=\"0.42777777777777776\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"width: 546px; height: 234px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQsetvrA0hh0W7ibWVlVaOTkNS0hkia6NA92sNCzsbPEbO93RHzho2HzWLxg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t洪昇是明朝遗民，《长恨歌》描绘的国家板荡，无不昭示着中国大明江山的哀荣，</span><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">这部神话色彩的帝王言情剧也有了历史的厚重感</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。再加上洪昉思自通音律，曲辞雅正，审慎的创作态度更是增色不少。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t我们的大作家又在《弹词》中描绘了玄宗痛失爱侣的孤寂：</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t破不刺马嵬驿舍，冷清清佛堂倒斜。一代红颜为君绝，千秋遗恨滴罗巾血。半棵树是薄命碑碣，一抔土是断肠墓穴。再无人过荒凉野，莽天涯谁吊梨花谢！可怜那抱幽怨的孤魂，只伴着呜咽咽的望帝悲声啼夜月。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t「家家收拾起，户户不提防」，在洪昇的笔下，唐玄宗不再是好色的皇帝，而杨贵妃不再是爱慕虚荣的「祸水」，他们有真挚的爱情。史料也表明唐玄宗自天宝四载（745）纳太真为妃，已再无子嗣，变相证明了他的专情。李杨甚至成了民间伉俪的楷模！《长生殿》至情至性，为空前绝后之不朽巨作！</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><img data-ratio=\"0.667621776504298\" data-type=\"other\" data-w=\"1047\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz/9NibN0rqxGDicWp3P6ZvQT82zTh0YamQseWE9NR2gc7OopibBHkewNVWiah6joYZPoAdEqMrrdt7DPkPQkiagoC7iakQ/640?wx_fmt=other\" style=\"max-width: 600px\"></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\"><br></span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(171, 25, 66);\">1688年，《长生殿》终于定稿，至此，李隆基杨玉环的故事完成了近千年自丑闻到楷模的嬗变</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">。后世虽有增益删削但不离洪子窠臼！不管是梅兰芳先生的代表剧目《贵妃醉酒》，还是日本在1955年移花接木式的电影《杨贵妃》，都更多地对二人予以赞美和同情。</span></p><p>\t</p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t「诗缘情而绮靡」，岂止是诗，所有的文艺作品都围绕着一个「情」字，我们梳理唐玄宗杨贵妃情事的脉络，得出波浪形的评价正弦曲线，也是要验证——</span></p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(38, 38, 38);\">\t「要使情留万古无穷！」</span></p><p>\t</p><p style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1.75em;\"><br></p><section style=\"font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;text-align: justify;margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: normal;\"><span
